DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `admin_website`;
CREATE TABLE `admin_website` (
  `website_id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `website_name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `website_link` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `note` text NOT NULL,
  `key_googleapi` text NOT NULL,
  `cse_googleapi` text NOT NULL,
  `delete_status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`website_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `biodata`;
CREATE TABLE `biodata` (
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `namaawal` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `namaakhir` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `phone_number` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `level` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `catatan` text NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`user_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `rating`;
CREATE TABLE `rating` (
  `rating_id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `website_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `rating` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `category_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `delete_status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`rating_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
